000108a0                    Flags 176552060
000108a4        Script --function <guid>( self, event, vars, sharedvars, globalvars, deltaTime )
do
	InitVars(vars, "MudAccum", 0)
	
	if (event == "OnMud") then
		vars.MudAccum =  vars.MudAccum + self.OnMudAmount
		if vars.MudAccum > 1.0 then vars.MudAccum = 1.0 end
		self.Mud = vars.MudAccum
		
	else
		local MUD_PER_METER = 0.1
		local WATER_FADE_OUT_TIME = 2.0
		local RAIN_FADE_OUT_TIME = 60.0
		local VELOCITY_THRESHOLD = 0.1 -- do not integrate when player is standing still
	
		-- handle non-boolean inputs possibly being nil
		velocity = self.Velocity
		if not velocity then velocity = 0 end
		
		targetMud = self.TargetMud
		if not targetMud then targetMud = 0 end
		
		rain = self.Rain
		if not rain then rain = 0 end
		
		if (self.IsSwimming) then
			vars.MudAccum = vars.MudAccum - deltaTime / WATER_FADE_OUT_TIME
			if (vars.MudAccum < 0) then vars.MudAccum = 0 end
		
		elseif (rain > 0) then
			vars.MudAccum = vars.MudAccum - deltaTime / RAIN_FADE_OUT_TIME
			if (vars.MudAccum < 0) then vars.MudAccum = 0 end			
		
		elseif (self.IsProne and velocity > VELOCITY_THRESHOLD and not self.IsVaulting) then -- player will be both prone and vaulting when vaulting
			if (targetMud > vars.MudAccum) then
				vars.MudAccum = vars.MudAccum + deltaTime * self.Velocity * MUD_PER_METER
				if vars.MudAccum > targetMud then vars.MudAccum = targetMud end
			end
		else
		end
		
		self.Mud = vars.MudAccum
	end
end
